# Establish a connection - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Ethereum, Monad, Base, and Polygon

Establish a connection

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [Connect](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection#connect)
    
*   [Disconnect](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection#disconnect)
    
*   [Change accounts](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection#change-accounts)
    

Once an application has [detected the provider](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/detecting-the-provider)
, it can then request to connect to Phantom. This connection request will prompt the user for permission to share their public key, indicating that they are willing to interact further. Users must approve a connection request before the app can make additional requests such as [signing a message](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/signing-a-message)
 or [sending a transaction](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/sending-a-transaction)
. Once permission is established for the first time, the web application’s domain will be whitelisted for future connection requests. After a connection is established, it is possible to terminate the connection from both the application and the user side.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection#connect)

Connect
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The default way to connect to Phantom is by calling `window.ethereum.request()` function.

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    const provider = getProvider(); // see "Detecting the Provider"
    try {
        const accounts = await provider.request({ method: "eth_requestAccounts" });
        console.log(accounts[0]);
        // 0x534583cd8cE0ac1af4Ce01Ae4f294d52b4Cd305F
    } catch (err) {
        // { code: 4001, message: 'User rejected the request.' }
    }
    

The `eth_requestAccounts` method will return a [Promise](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Promise)
. If it resolves, it is an array where the connected address is in the 0th index, and rejects (throw when awaited) when the user declines the request or closes the pop-up. See [Errors](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/errors)
 for a breakdown of error messages Phantom may emit. When the user accepts the request to connect, the provider will also emit a `connect` event that contains the `chainId` of the network the user is connected to.

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    provider.on("connect", (connectionInfo: { chainId: string }) => console.log(`Connected to chain: ${connectionInfo.chainId}`));
    

Once the web application is connected to Phantom, it will be able to read the connected account’s address and prompt the user for additional transactions. It also exposes a convenience `isConnected` boolean.

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    console.log(provider.selectedAddress);
    // 0x534583cd8cE0ac1af4Ce01Ae4f294d52b4Cd305F 
    console.log(provider.isConnected());
    // true
    

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection#disconnect)

Disconnect
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There is no way to programmatically disconnect a user from their connection once they have established one.  
  
Once a user has established a connection, Phantom will add the website they opened a connection with to a list of “trusted apps.” The user can then revoke access through the UI at any time, and will then need to reconnect. Phantom will attempt to reconnect to any application that is added to the users’ “trusted apps” automatically.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection#change-accounts)

Change accounts
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Phantom allows users to seamlessly manage multiple accounts (addresses) from within a single extension or mobile app. Whenever a user switches accounts, Phantom will emit an `accountsChanged` event. If a user changes accounts while already connected to an application, and the new account had already whitelisted that application, then the user will stay connected and Phantom will pass the public key of the new account:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    provider.on('accountsChanged', (publicKeys: String[]) => {
        if (publicKeys) {
            // Set new public key and continue as usual
            console.log(`Switched to account ${publicKeys[0]}`);
        } 
    });
    

If Phantom does not pass the public key of the new account, an application can either do nothing or attempt to reconnect:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    provider.on('accountsChanged', (publicKeys: String[]) => {
        if (publicKeys) {
          // Set new public key and continue as usual
          console.log(`Switched to account ${publicKeys[0].toBase58()}`);
        } else {
          // Attempt to reconnect to Phantom
          provider.request({ method: "eth_requestAccounts" }).catch((error) => {
            // handle connection failure
          });
        }
    });
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Detect the provider](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/detecting-the-provider)
[Send a transaction](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/sending-a-transaction)

⌘I

# Error messages and codes - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/provider-api-reference/errors#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Provider API reference

Error messages and codes

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

When making requests to Phantom in [establishing a connection](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/establishing-a-connection)
, [sending a transaction](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/sending-a-transaction)
, or [signing a message](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/signing-a-message)
, Phantom may respond with an error. The following is a list of all possible error codes and their meanings. These error messages follow [EIP-1474](https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-1474#error-codes)
 and [EIP-1193](https://eips.ethereum.org/EIPS/eip-1193#provider-errors)
.

| Code | Title | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 4900 | Disconnected | Phantom could not connect to the network. |
| 4100 | Unauthorized | The requested method and/or account has not been authorized by the user. |
| 4001 | User Rejected Request | The user rejected the request through Phantom. |
| \-32000 | Invalid Input | Missing or invalid parameters. |
| \-32002 | Requested resource not available | This error occurs when a dapp attempts to submit a new transaction while Phantom’s approval dialog is already open for a previous transaction. Only one approve window can be open at a time. Users should approve or reject their transaction before initiating a new transaction. |
| \-32003 | Transaction Rejected | Phantom does not recognize a valid transaction. |
| \-32601 | Method Not Found | Phantom does not recognize the method. |
| \-32603 | Internal Error | Something went wrong within Phantom. |

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[request](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/provider-api-reference/methods/request)
[Get started with Bitcoin](https://docs.phantom.com/bitcoin/integrating-phantom)

# Transaction Validation - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/lighthouse#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Security and validation

Transaction Validation

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [What this means for your transactions](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/lighthouse#what-this-means-for-your-transactions)
    
*   [Additional information](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/lighthouse#additional-information)
    

When building with Phantom, you may see transactions that include Lighthouse assertion instructions. Lighthouse is a Solana program that adds runtime checks to transactions. These checks validate onchain state and will cause the transaction to fail if conditions aren’t met. These assertions are included to ensure user safety by protecting against unexpected outcomes like simulation spoofing or malicious transaction manipulation.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/lighthouse#what-this-means-for-your-transactions)

What this means for your transactions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you submit a transaction to Phantom, it may be augmented with Lighthouse assertion instructions before being submitted to the network. This means that if you’re checking transactions onchain as part of your confirmation flow, you should be aware that the transaction onchain will be different from what you originally submitted. Additionally, these assertions can cause a transaction to fail even when it would otherwise execute successfully. For example, if a swap transaction includes an assertion checking for a specific token balance and the actual balance differs, the entire transaction will fail. You don’t need to do anything special to handle these assertions. They’re included in the transaction by Phantom and are processed automatically onchain.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/lighthouse#additional-information)

Additional information
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For guidance on handling transaction warnings and best practices, see [Domain and transaction warnings](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Domain and transaction warnings](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings)
[Token pages](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/token-pages)

⌘I

# Phantom deep links - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/deeplinks-ios-and-android#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Mobile deep links

Phantom deep links

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

As of Phantom `v22.04.11`, iOS and Android apps can now natively interact with Phantom through either [universal links](https://developer.apple.com/ios/universal-links/)
 (recommended) or [deeplinks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mobile_deep_linking)
. We refer to both of these workflows collectively as “deeplinks”. Currently only Solana is supported for deeplinks. All [provider methods](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/README)
 follow a protocol format of:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/<version>/<method>
    

It is also possible (but not recommended) to call these methods using Phantom’s custom protocol handler:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    phantom://<version>/<method>
    

In addition to these provider methods, Phantom also supports [other methods](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/README)
 that are accessible via deeplinks. Specifically, users can open web apps within Phantom’s in-app browser via the [Browse](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse)
 deeplink.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Handle sessions](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/handling-sessions)

# Encryption - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Mobile deep links

Encryption

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [Encryption and decryption workflow](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#encryption-and-decryption-workflow)
    
*   [Connect](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#connect)
    
*   [Subsequent deeplinks](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#subsequent-deeplinks)
    
*   [Encryption resources](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#encryption-resources)
    
*   [JavaScript](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#javascript)
    
*   [iOS](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#ios)
    
*   [Android](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#android)
    

Deeplinks are encrypted using symmetric key encryption generated from a [Diffie-Hellman key exchange](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Diffie%E2%80%93Hellman_key_exchange)
. While deeplink sessions will be created in plaintext, an encrypted channel will be created to prevent session tokens from getting hijacked.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#encryption-and-decryption-workflow)

Encryption and decryption workflow
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Phantom deeplinks are encrypted with the following workflows:

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#connect)

Connect

1.  **\[dapp\]:** On the initial [connect deeplink](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/connect)
    , dapps should include a `dapp_encryption_public_key` query parameter. It’s recommended to create a new x25519 keypair for every session started with `connect`. In all methods, the public key for this keypair is referred to as `dapp_encryption_public_key`.
2.  **\[phantom\]:** Upon handling a `connect` deeplink, Phantom will also generate a new x25519 keypair.
    *   Phantom will return this public key as `phantom_encryption_public_key` in the `connect` response.
    *   Phantom will create a secret key using Diffie-Hellman with `dapp_encryption_public_key` and the _**private key**_ associated with `phantom_encryption_public_key`.
    *   Phantom will locally store a mapping of `dapp_encryption_public_key` to shared secrets for use with decryption in subsequent deeplinks.
3.  **\[dapp\]:** Upon receiving the `connect` response, the dapp should create a shared secret by using Diffie-Hellman with `phantom_encryption_public_key` and the _**private key**_ associated with `dapp_encryption_public_key`. This shared secret should then be used to decrypt the `data` field in the response. If done correctly, the user’s public key will be available to share with the dapp inside the `data` JSON object.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#subsequent-deeplinks)

Subsequent deeplinks

1.  **\[dapp\]:** For any subsequent methods (such as [SignTransaction](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/signtransaction)
     and [SignMessage](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/signmessage)
    ), dapps should send a `dapp_encryption_public_key` (the public key side of the shared secret) used with Phantom along with an encrypted `payload` object.
2.  **\[phantom\]:** Upon approval, Phantom will encrypt the signed response as a JSON object with the encryption sent as a `data=` query param.
3.  **\[dapp\]:** Upon receiving the deeplink response, dapps should decrypt the object in the `data=` query param to view the signature.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#encryption-resources)

Encryption resources
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To learn more about encryption and decryption, please refer to the following libraries:

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#javascript)

JavaScript

[TweetNaCl.js](https://github.com/dchest/tweetnacl-js)

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#ios)

iOS

[TweetNaCl SwiftWrap](https://github.com/bitmark-inc/tweetnacl-swiftwrap)

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption#android)

Android

*   [Tink](https://github.com/google/tink)
    
*   [TweetNaCl Java](https://github.com/InstantWebP2P/tweetnacl-java)
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Specifying redirects](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects)
[Limitations](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/limitations)

⌘I

# Specifying redirects - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Mobile deep links

Specifying redirects

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [Redirect link types](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects#redirect-link-types)
    
*   [HTTPS URLs](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects#https-urls)
    
*   [Custom scheme URIs](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects#custom-scheme-uris)
    

All [methods](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/README)
 support a `redirect_link=` param that lets Phantom know how to get back to the original app. The URI specified by this param should be URL encoded. If the deeplink request to Phantom comes with a response, Phantom will append the results as query parameters in the `redirect_link=` upon redirecting.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects#redirect-link-types)

Redirect link types
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use either HTTPS URLs or custom scheme URIs for `redirect_link`, but each has different behavior:

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects#https-urls)

HTTPS URLs

When using an HTTPS URL (e.g., `https://yourapp.com/callback`):

*   **App metadata displays correctly**: Logo, title, and favicon are fetched and shown in the connection approval dialog
*   **Opens in browser**: The redirect opens in the mobile browser instead of redirecting back to your app

Example:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    redirect_link=https%3A%2F%2Fyourapp.com%2Fcallback
    

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/specifying-redirects#custom-scheme-uris)

Custom scheme URIs

When using a custom scheme URI (e.g., `mydapp://onPhantomConnected`):

*   **Redirects back to app**: Properly redirects back to your mobile app
*   **No app metadata**: Logo, title, and favicon are not displayed in the connection approval dialog

Example:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    redirect_link%3Dmydapp%3A%2F%2FonPhantomConnected
    

After redirect with response data:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    redirect_link=mydapp://onPhantomConnected?data=...
    

**Choosing a redirect link type**:

*   Use **HTTPS URLs** if displaying your app’s branding in the connection dialog is important, but be aware that users will be redirected to the browser instead of your app.
*   Use **custom scheme URIs** if seamless app redirection is critical, but note that your app’s branding will not appear in the connection dialog.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Handle sessions](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/handling-sessions)
[Encryption](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/encryption)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Navigation

Security and validation

Domain and transaction warnings

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [New domain warning](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings#new-domain-warning)
    
*   [Transaction simulation warning](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings#transaction-simulation-warning)
    
*   [Prediction market token burn warning](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings#prediction-market-token-burn-warning)
    

Phantom may display different warnings when users connect to your app or sign transactions. These warnings are designed to help protect users from unexpected or unsafe activity.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings#new-domain-warning)

New domain warning
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your app or website has been newly launched, Phantom may show users the following message:

> _“This domain is new or has not been reviewed yet. Proceed with caution.”_

![Warning message shown when connecting to a new or unverified domain](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/-BstuKpEdI9oFGb0/images/warning-new-domain-dev-docs.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-BstuKpEdI9oFGb0&q=85&s=10f0312745d24d90e7eac0e8484083b5 "Warning message shown when connecting to a new or unverified domain") This warning appears automatically for newly detected domains and typically disappears after a few days once the domain has been reviewed. There’s usually **no action required** on your part. If the warning remains visible for more than a week, contact our domain review team using this [form](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1JgIxdmolgh_80xMfQKBKx9-QPC7LRdN6LHpFFW8BlKM/viewform)
.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings#transaction-simulation-warning)

Transaction simulation warning
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If Phantom can’t accurately simulate a transaction before it’s sent, users may see the following message:

> _“This dApp could be malicious. Do not proceed unless you are certain it is safe.”_

![Warning displayed when Phantom can’t confirm the safety of a transaction](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/-BstuKpEdI9oFGb0/images/warning-malicious-dapp-devdocs.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-BstuKpEdI9oFGb0&q=85&s=a09ae7944dbcc318f8823125e08a15cf "Warning displayed when Phantom can’t confirm the safety of a transaction") This message appears when Phantom is unable to safely predict a transaction’s outcome before execution. If Phantom displays this warning when you sign a transaction on your domain, follow these steps:

*   Limit the transaction to **one** signer.
*   If the transaction requires multiple signers, sign it with Phantom first using [signTransaction](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/sending-a-transaction#sign-a-transaction-without-sending)
     instead of signAndSendTransaction, then collect signatures from the other signers.
*   If your transaction approaches Solana’s size limit, split it into multiple signing requests or use [Address Lookup Tables](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/sending-a-transaction-1#build-an-address-lut)
    .
*   Before submitting the transaction for signing, simulate the transaction with `sigVerify: false` using your RPC node to ensure they will not fail onchain. Failed transactions could trigger simulation warnings.

If you’ve made these changes and the warning persists, or if you can’t apply these changes, contact our domain review team using this [form](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1JgIxdmolgh_80xMfQKBKx9-QPC7LRdN6LHpFFW8BlKM/viewform)
.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/domain-and-transaction-warnings#prediction-market-token-burn-warning)

Prediction market token burn warning
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If a transaction attempts to burn a prediction market token, Phantom may show users the following message:

> _“This transaction will burn a valuable prediction market token. Please use the Phantom app to close the position first.”_

This warning appears when Phantom detects a transaction that would permanently burn a prediction market token. To resolve this warning, contact our Trust and Safety team using this [form](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/1JgIxdmolgh_80xMfQKBKx9-QPC7LRdN6LHpFFW8BlKM/viewform)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[MCP server](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/mcp-server)
[Transaction Validation](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/lighthouse)

⌘I

# Create an app - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-app#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Account setup

Create an app

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [Create an app](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-app#create-an-app)
    
*   [Next steps](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-app#next-steps)
    

After creating your Phantom Portal account, the next step is to create an app. This establishes your app’s presence in the portal and allows you to configure settings, verify your domain, and integrate with Phantom.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-app#create-an-app)

Create an app
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you first sign in to Phantom Portal, you’ll see an option to create a new app.

1.  Click **Create New App** or **Add App** on your dashboard.
2.  Fill in the required fields:
    *   **Upload Avatar**: Upload your app icon (PNG or JPG, max 1MB, 250×250px minimum)
    *   **App Name**: Enter your app’s official name
    *   **Website**: Enter your app’s public URL (must use HTTPS, e.g., `https://yourapp.com`)
3.  Click **Continue**.

![Create New App modal showing app creation form](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/oGAeqebvkE4mhDv1/phantom-portal/images/create-app.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oGAeqebvkE4mhDv1&q=85&s=d010fd338928ad9fab884cf044efa6ab) Your app is now created and you can proceed with the setup process. You’ll be taken to your app’s dashboard where you can:

*   Verify your domain (required for SDK usage and app display)
*   Configure allowed origins for your app
*   Add additional app information and branding
*   Get your App ID for SDK integration

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-app#next-steps)

Next steps
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

-----------------\
\
Previous: Sign up for a Phantom Portal account to manage your app](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-account)
[Verify your domain\
------------------\
\
Next: Verify your domain for SDK usage and app display](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/verify-domain)

# Configure allowed origins and redirect URLs - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Account setup

Configure allowed origins and redirect URLs

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [Allowed origins](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#allowed-origins)
    
*   [Add allowed origins](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#add-allowed-origins)
    
*   [Allowed origin requirements](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#allowed-origin-requirements)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#examples)
    
*   [Redirect URLs](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#redirect-urls)
    
*   [Add redirect URLs](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#add-redirect-urls)
    
*   [Redirect URL requirements](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#redirect-url-requirements)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#examples-2)
    
*   [Common setup mistakes](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#common-setup-mistakes)
    
*   [Need help?](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#need-help)
    
*   [Next steps](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#next-steps)
    

To use Phantom Connect in development and production, you must configure _allowed origins_ and _redirect URLs_ in Phantom Portal. These settings tell Phantom where your app is allowed to run and where users can be redirected after authentication. Both are required to connect users.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#allowed-origins)

Allowed origins
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Allowed origins define _where your app is allowed to initiate a connection_ from. Phantom will only connect if the request comes from one of these domains. This prevents other websites from impersonating your app.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#add-allowed-origins)

Add allowed origins

1.  In Phantom Portal, expand your app in the left navigation and select **Set Up**.
2.  Scroll to **Allowed Origins**.
3.  Enter a domain where your app runs.
4.  Select **Add**.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#allowed-origin-requirements)

Allowed origin requirements

*   Include the protocol (`https://` for production).
*   Use exact domains only.
*   Do not include paths, query strings, or wildcards.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#examples)

Examples

| Environment | Example |
| --- | --- |
| Production | `https://yourapp.com` |
| Staging | `https://staging.yourapp.com` |
| Local development | `http://localhost:3000` |

If your app runs in multiple environments, add _each origin_ separately.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#redirect-urls)

Redirect URLs
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Redirect URLs define _where users are sent after authentication_. These are required for social login flows (Google, Apple) and for completing the Phantom Connect handshake. Redirect URLs can be web URLs or mobile app URIs.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#add-redirect-urls)

Add redirect URLs

1.  In Phantom Portal, expand your app in the left navigation and select **Set Up**.
2.  Scroll to **Redirect URLs**.
3.  Enter a valid redirect URL.
4.  Select **Add**.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#redirect-url-requirements)

Redirect URL requirements

*   Must exactly match the URL used in your app.
*   Must be added and allowlisted in Phantom Portal before you can use it in production.
*   Multiple redirect URLs are allowed.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#examples-2)

Examples

| Use case | Example |
| --- | --- |
| Web app | `https://yourapp.com/auth/callback` |
| Local development | `http://localhost:3000/auth/callback` |
| Mobile app | `myapp://phantom-auth-callback` |

When using Google or Apple login, users are redirected to one of these URLs after authentication. If the redirect URL is missing or mismatched, login will fail.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#common-setup-mistakes)

Common setup mistakes
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Adding a redirect URL but forgetting to add the corresponding allowed origin.
*   Including paths or wildcards in allowed origins.
*   Using a redirect URL in code that hasn’t been added to Phantom Portal.
*   Using `http://` for production domains.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#need-help)

Need help?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Contact [Phantom developer support](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSeHWETFkEJbHQCF-lnl1AHmVQPuyfC0HbnxjDjIp6VYV1sBZQ/viewform)
.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/configure-urls#next-steps)

Next steps
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Verify your domain\
------------------\
\
Previous: Verify your domain](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/verify-domain)
[Edit app info\
-------------\
\
Next: Add your app information](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info)

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Verify your domain](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/verify-domain)
[Add your app information](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info)

⌘I

# AI-assisted development - Phantom developer documentation

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Developer tools

AI-assisted development

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)

On this page

Your AI coding assistant can search Phantom documentation directly, giving you accurate, up-to-date guidance while you build.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#ai-tools)

AI tools
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[MCP server\
----------\
\
Connect Cursor, VS Code, Claude, or Claude Code to search our docs in real-time](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/mcp-server)
[Cursor AI prompts\
-----------------\
\
One-shot prompts that generate complete, production-ready SDK implementations](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/cursor-prompts)

**ChatGPT integration**: Every documentation page includes an “Open in ChatGPT” button in the contextual menu for quick implementation help.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#mcp-server)

MCP server
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Phantom MCP (Model Context Protocol) server enables AI coding assistants to search and retrieve information from the Phantom developer documentation. This allows your AI assistant to provide accurate, up-to-date guidance when building Phantom integrations.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#setup)

Setup

| Tool | One-click | Manual |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Cursor | Click “Connect to Cursor” on any docs page | Add to `~/.cursor/mcp.json` |
| VS Code | Click “Connect to VS Code” | Add to `.vscode/mcp.json` |
| Claude.ai | —   | Add connector in Settings |
| Claude Code | —   | `claude mcp add --transport http phantom-docs https://docs.phantom.com/mcp` |

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#configuration)

Configuration

Add this configuration to your MCP settings:

mcp.json

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      "mcpServers": {
        "phantom-docs": {
          "type": "sse",
          "url": "https://docs.phantom.com/mcp"
        }
      }
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#example-prompts)

Example prompts

Once configured, try asking your AI assistant:

*   “How do I set up Phantom Connect in a React app?”
*   “Show me how to sign a message with the Browser SDK.”
*   “What’s the process for verifying a domain in Phantom Portal?”
*   “How do I handle transaction errors in React Native?”

[Full MCP server documentation\
-----------------------------\
\
Complete setup guides for all supported tools](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/mcp-server)

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#cursor-ai-prompts)

Cursor AI prompts
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use one-shot prompts with Cursor AI to generate complete, production-ready Phantom SDK implementations. These prompts create full applications with wallet connection, message signing, and transaction handling.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#available-prompts)

Available prompts

| SDK | What it generates |
| --- | --- |
| React SDK | Complete app with wallet connection, message signing, SOL transfers |
| React Native SDK | Mobile app with Expo, OAuth flow, native wallet functionality |
| Browser SDK | Vanilla JS implementation for any web framework |

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#how-to-use)

How to use

1

[](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#)

Get App ID from Phantom Portal

Visit [Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/get-app-id)
 to get your App ID before using any prompt.

2

[](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#)

Copy prompt for your SDK

Open the [Cursor AI prompts page](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/cursor-prompts)
 and copy the prompt for your preferred SDK (React, React Native, or Browser).

3

[](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#)

Replace placeholders

Replace `[YOUR_APP_ID]` and `[YOUR_REDIRECT_URL]` (or `[YOUR_SCHEME]` for React Native) with your actual values.

4

[](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#)

Paste into Cursor

Open Cursor AI, press `Cmd+K` (or `Ctrl+K` on Windows), and paste the complete prompt.

5

[](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#)

Review and run

Cursor will generate a full implementation. Review the code, then run and test your integration.

[View all Cursor prompts\
-----------------------\
\
Get prompts for React, React Native, and Browser SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/cursor-prompts)

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#best-practices)

Best practices
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#provide-context)

Provide context

Give your AI assistant enough context to generate accurate code. Include:

*   Your target framework (React, React Native, or vanilla JS).
*   Specific features you need (wallet connection, transactions, message signing).
*   General app structure and requirements.

**Security best practice**: Avoid sharing sensitive information like App IDs, redirect URLs, or API keys with AI assistants. Use placeholders like `[YOUR_APP_ID]` in prompts, then replace them with actual values in your code after generation.

**Example of a good prompt:**

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    I'm building a React app with Phantom Connect. I need to:
    1. Connect a wallet using social login
    2. Sign messages for authentication
    3. Send SOL transactions
    
    I'll replace [YOUR_APP_ID] and [YOUR_REDIRECT_URL] placeholders with my actual values after the code is generated.
    

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#combine-tools)

Combine tools

Use MCP server for questions and documentation lookups, then use Cursor prompts for scaffolding complete implementations:

1.  **Ask questions first**: Use MCP server to understand concepts (“How does Phantom Connect authentication work?”).
2.  **Generate code**: Use Cursor prompts to scaffold your implementation.
3.  **Refine with MCP**: Ask follow-up questions to customize the generated code.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#verify-generated-code)

Verify generated code

Always review AI-generated code before deploying:

*   Check App ID matches your Phantom Portal app.
*   Verify redirect URLs are allowlisted in Phantom Portal.
*   Ensure error handling is present for all async operations.
*   Confirm lamports are calculated correctly (1 SOL = 1,000,000,000 lamports).
*   Test wallet connection flow end-to-end.
*   Validate transaction amounts and recipient addresses.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/ai-tools#resources)

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\
Complete setup guides for Cursor, VS Code, Claude, and Claude Code](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/mcp-server)

\
Example implementations and starter templates](https://docs.phantom.com/resources/recipes)

--------------------\
\
Choose the right SDK for your application](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)

# Send a transaction - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/sending-a-transaction#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Ethereum, Monad, Base, and Polygon

Send a transaction

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

Once a web application is connected to Phantom, it can prompt the user for permission to send transactions on their behalf. To send a transaction, you will need to have a valid transaction object. It should look a little like this:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    {
      from: "0xEA674fdDe714fd979de3EdF0F56AA9716B898ec8",
      to: "0xac03bb73b6a9e108530aff4df5077c2b3d481e5a",
      gasLimit: "21000",
      maxFeePerGas: "300",
      maxPriorityFeePerGas: "10",
      nonce: "0",
      value: "10000000000"
    }
    

However, this transaction object needs to be signed using the sender’s private key. This ensures that only the person that holds the private key can send transactions from the public address. To prompt Phantom to send a transaction to the network, refer to the following code snippet:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    const result = await provider.request({
      method: 'eth_sendTransaction',
      params: [        \
                {\
                from: accounts[0],\
                to: '0x0c54FcCd2e384b4BB6f2E405Bf5Cbc15a017AaFb',\
                value: '0x0',\
                gasLimit: '0x5028',\
                gasPrice: '0x2540be400',\
                type: '0x0',\
              },\
            ],
    });
    

This is the building blocks of what you will need to send a transaction. However, if you were to copy/paste this, it would likely fail. There are several pieces of a transaction that are best provided in a dynamic manner. For details, refer to the [sendTransaction](https://github.com/phantom-labs/eth_sandbox/blob/main/src/utils/sendTransaction.ts)
 function in our sandbox.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

Navigation

Testing and debugging

Mobile web debugging

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [iOS](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/mobile-web-debugging#ios)
    
*   [Android](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/mobile-web-debugging#android)
    

Watch [How to debug your dapp on iPhone using Phantom](https://www.loom.com/share/1b1817d84af649c9a38e5dbd8ed25ca9?t=1)
 on loom.

Developers can debug their mobile web dapps using PC browsers. To enable this in Phantom mobile, go to **Settings** > **Developer Settings**, and toggle **Web View Debugging** on. Then follow the steps for your platform.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/mobile-web-debugging#ios)

iOS
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Tether your iPhone to your computer via USB.
2.  On your iPhone go to **Settings** > **Safari** > **Advanced** and turn on **Web Inspector**.
3.  On your computer open Safari. Then from the menu bar **Safari** > Settings -> Advanced tab -> turn on **Show features for web developers**.
4.  Open your web dapp in Phantom on your tethered device.
5.  Back on your computer from the Safari menu bar, go to **Develop** > \[Your device\] > \[Your dapp\].

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/mobile-web-debugging#android)

Android
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Tether your Android phone to your computer via USB.
2.  Open your web dapp in Phantom on your tethered device.
3.  On your computer open `chrome://inspect/#devices` on Chrome.
4.  Select your device on the left and select **Inspect** on the Phantom dapp contents you’d like to inspect.

![Developer Settings menu in the Phantom browser extension](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/developer-powertools/images/developer-settings-web.avif?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=57759c4e5f823d59bd38729395ecd62e) For more information, see [React Native WebView debugging guide](https://github.com/react-native-webview/react-native-webview/blob/master/docs/Debugging.md#debugging-webview-contents)
.

YesNo

You need a Phantom Portal account to register your app, configure settings, and manage its presence in Phantom. This page explains how to sign up and access the dashboard.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-account#sign-up-to-create-your-account)

Sign up to create your account
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Phantom Portal uses social login for secure, password-free access.

1.  Go to [phantom.app/portal](https://phantom.app/portal)
    .
2.  Click **Sign Up**.
3.  Sign in with your Google account or Apple ID.

Your Phantom Portal account is created automatically.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/create-account#phantom-portal-dashboard)

Phantom Portal dashboard
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you sign in, you’ll see the main dashboard, which includes:

*   **Set Up**: App ID, SDK installation, allowed origins, and redirect URLs
*   **Edit App Info**: App details and branding
*   **Contracts**: Auto-Confirm contract submissions

![Main Phantom Portal dashboard view](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/oGAeqebvkE4mhDv1/phantom-portal/images/portal-dashboard.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oGAeqebvkE4mhDv1&q=85&s=f12e33ee584ec9b1f69c4af6a248e116)

# Add your app information - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

⌘KAsk AI

Navigation

Account setup

Add your app information

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [Add your app information](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#add-your-app-information)
    
*   [App access control](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#app-access-control)
    
*   [Domain verification](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#domain-verification)
    
*   [Submit for review](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#submit-for-review)
    
*   [Next steps](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#next-steps)
    

Fill out more information about your app and add graphics to customize how the app appears to users in Phantom. Any changes you make on the **Edit App Info** page will go through a review process. Once approved by Phantom, they will be published across all platforms. ![Edit app info page showing all fields](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/oGAeqebvkE4mhDv1/phantom-portal/images/app-info-form.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=oGAeqebvkE4mhDv1&q=85&s=05f3944a58da1a1a3cfe86aceab7e131)

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#add-your-app-information)

Add your app information
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  In Phantom Portal, expand your app in the main nagivation, then click **Edit App Info**.
2.  App Details:
    *   App icon: Upload an icon as a PNG or JPG image, up to 250×250px and 1MB.
    *   Name: Enter your app’s official name (up to 50 characters).
    *   Description: Provide a brief tagline describing what your app does (up to 100 characters). The description field can accommodate longer text, but descriptions over 100 characters may not display well in the app.
    *   Public URL: Your app’s public URL within Phantom, must use HTTPS. You will need to verify your domain to use Phantom Connect SDK and for your app to be visible in Phantom’s **Explore** tab.
    *   Cover image: A PNG or JPG image, recommended 1500×500px, up to 2MB.
3.  Categories:
    *   Category: Select the category that best represents your app (AI, DeFi, NFT, gaming, and others).
    *   Networks: Select all blockchain networks your app supports.
4.  Social Links: Add links to your website, Discord, Telegram, GitHub, X (Twitter), and YouTube.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#app-access-control)

App access control
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your app’s access mode controls who can connect:

*   **DISABLED**: App is banned, no users can connect
*   **PRIVATE**: Invited team members only (max 20) — this is the default mode
*   **PUBLIC**: All users can connect — available after Phantom approval

In PRIVATE mode, you must invite team members through Phantom Portal. If someone who isn’t invited tries to connect, the connection is rejected.

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#domain-verification)

Domain verification

Domain verification is required to use Phantom Connect SDK and for your app to appear in Phantom’s **Explore** tab and search results:

1.  In Phantom Portal, click **Verify now**.
2.  Add a DNS TXT record to your domain with the details on the screen.
3.  Copy the verification code from Phantom Portal.
4.  Select **Verify Domain** in Phantom Portal.

DNS configuration:

| Field | Value |
| --- | --- |
| **Type** | TXT |
| **Host** | `@` |
| **Value** | Verification code from Phantom Portal |
| **TTL** | 3600 |

[View the detailed verification guide →](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/verify-domain)

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#submit-for-review)

Submit for review
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After making any changes to your app information, a **Submit changes for review** button will appear above the cover image section. Click this button to submit your updates for review by the Phantom team.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/edit-app-info#next-steps)

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\

[Get App ID and integrate\
------------------------\
\
Next: Get your App ID and start building](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/get-app-id)

# Solana Actions and Blinks - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/solana-actions-and-blinks#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Solana features

Solana Actions and Blinks

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

Watch [Solana Actions and Blinks](https://youtu.be/TU87JjHxQQo)
 demo on YouTube.

[Solana Actions](https://solana.com/docs/advanced/actions)
 are APIs to deliver signable transactions from a variety of web contexts. Blockchain links, or [Blinks](https://solana.com/docs/advanced/actions#blinks)
, are client applications that introspect Action APIs and construct user interfaces to interact with Actions. The Phantom Extension supports rendering Blinks on Twitter/X.com. If an Action URL is posted to Twitter/X.com, the Phantom extension is can construct a UI to interact with the transaction from directly within the user’s timeline. This feature is disabled by default. Users can opt-in to enabling this feature via by goint to **Settings** > **Experimental Features** and turning on **Blinks**. Phantom will only render Actions that are registered under the Dialect-maintained [Actions Registry](https://solana.com/docs/advanced/actions#dialect's-actions-registry)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Solana Token Extensions (Token22)](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/solana-token-extensions-token22)
[Testnet mode](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/testnet-mode)

# Browse - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Other methods

Browse

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [URL structure](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse#url-structure)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse#parameters)
    
*   [Example](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse#example)
    

Deeplinks provide a convenient way for users to open web apps within Phantom. Using their phone’s camera, users can scan a QR code to open a page directly within Phantom’s in-app browser. If a web app detects that a user is on mobile, it can also prompt the user to open a specific page within Phantom’s in-app browser. The `browse` deeplink can be used before a [Connect](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/connect)
 event takes places, as it does not require a `session` param.

The `browse` deeplinks are not intended to be pasted into mobile web browsers. These deeplinks must either be handled by an app or clicked on by an end user.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse#url-structure)

URL structure
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/browse/<url>?ref=<ref>
    

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse#parameters)

Parameters
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `url` (required): The URL that should open within Phantom’s in-app browser, URL-encoded.
*   `ref` (required): The URL of the requesting app, URL-encoded.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/browse#example)

Example
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following is an example request to open an [NFT listed on Magic Eden](https://magiceden.io/item-details/8yjN8iRuoiYiKW487cnW9vn6mLBR5E8aCNKsBRmTP9vN)
:

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/browse/https%3A%2F%2Fmagiceden.io%2Fitem-details%2F8yjN8iRuoiYiKW487cnW9vn6mLBR5E8aCNKsBRmTP9vN?ref=https%3A%2F%2Fmagiceden.io

YesNo

[Fungible](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible)

# Sign a message - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/signing-a-message#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Ethereum, Monad, Base, and Polygon

Sign a message

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [Support for “Sign-In with” standards](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/signing-a-message#support-for-%E2%80%9Csign-in-with%E2%80%9D-standards)
    

When a web application is connected to Phantom, it can also request that the user signs a given message. Applications are free to write their own messages which will be displayed to users from within Phantom’s signature prompt. Message signatures do not involve network fees and are a convenient way for apps to verify ownership of an address. To learn how you can use libraries such as [ethers.js](https://docs.ethers.org/v5/)
 to abstract away some of these intricacies, see [handleSignMessage](https://github.com/phantom-labs/eth_sandbox/blob/main/src/App.tsx#L193-L211)
 in our sandbox.

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    const message = 'To avoid digital dognappers, sign below to authenticate with CryptoCorgis.';
    const from = accounts[0];
    const msg = `0x${Buffer.from(message, 'utf8').toString('hex')}`;
    const sign = await provider.request({
            method: 'personal_sign',
            params: [msg, from, 'Example password'],
        });
    

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/signing-a-message#support-for-%E2%80%9Csign-in-with%E2%80%9D-standards)

Support for “Sign-In with” standards
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Applications that rely on signing messages to authenticate users can choose to opt-in to one of the various “Sign-In with” (SIW) standards. For more details, see [Sign-In with (SIW) standards](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/signing-a-message)
.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Send a transaction](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/sending-a-transaction)
[Provider API reference](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/provider-api-reference/README)

⌘I

# Swap - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Other methods

Swap

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [URL structure](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#url-structure)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#parameters)
    
*   [Examples](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#examples)
    
*   [Swap SOL to WIF](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#swap-sol-to-wif)
    
*   [Bridge USDC on Solana to USDT on Ethereum](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#bridge-usdc-on-solana-to-usdt-on-ethereum)
    

Watch [Swap demo](https://youtu.be/qJNv7lpYmtw)
 on YouTube.

Phantom supports deeplinking directly to the in-app swapper. Developers can specify which tokens should be prefilled in the `buy` and `sell` fields. In addition to swapping tokens on a single chain, the swapper can also be used to bridge stablecoins across chains, such as USDT on Ethereum to USDC on Solana. The `swap` deeplink can be used at anytime. It does not need to be proceeded by a [Connect](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/connect)
 event, as it does not require a `session` param.

The `swap` deeplinks are not intended to be pasted into mobile web browsers. These deeplinks must either be handled by an app or tapped on by an end user.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#url-structure)

URL structure
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/v1/swap?buy=<buy>&sell=<sell>
    

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#parameters)

Parameters
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `buy`: The [CAIP-19](https://github.com/ChainAgnostic/CAIPs/blob/main/CAIPs/caip-19.md)
     address of the token that should be bought, URL-encoded. Defaults to SOL if omitted.
*   `sell`: The [CAIP-19](https://github.com/ChainAgnostic/CAIPs/blob/main/CAIPs/caip-19.md)
     address of the token that should be sold, URL-encoded. Defaults to SOL if omitted.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#examples)

Examples
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Using a mobile device, tap the following links to try out the `swap` deeplink:

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#swap-sol-to-wif)

Swap SOL to WIF

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/v1/swap/?buy=solana%3A101%2Faddress%3AEKpQGSJtjMFqKZ9KQanSqYXRcF8fBopzLHYxdM65zcjm&sell=
    

### 

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/swap#bridge-usdc-on-solana-to-usdt-on-ethereum)

Bridge USDC on Solana to USDT on Ethereum

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/v1/swap/?buy=eip155%3A1%2Faddress%3A0xdAC17F958D2ee523a2206206994597C13D831ec7&sell=solana%3A101%2Faddress%3AEPjFWdd5AufqSSqeM2qN1xzybapC8G4wEGGkZwyTDt1v
    

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Fungible](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible)
[Wallet Standard](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/wallet-standard)

# Events - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/provider-api-reference/events/README#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Events

Events

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

Phantom’s provider API available at `window.ethereum` implements a Node.js style [EventEmitter](https://nodejs.org/api/events.html)
 API, that allows you to hook into different events that are emitted upon certain actions that take place in either the dapp, or the wallet. Each page in this section will be an isolated piece of information that informs you of all the technical details you need to know about each event Phantom supports.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

Other methods

Fungible

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

On this page

*   [URL structure](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible#url-structure)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible#parameters)
    
*   [Example](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible#example)
    

Phantom supports deeplinking directly to a fungible token detail page. Developers can specify which chain and token detail page to navigate to. The `fungible` deeplink can be used at anytime. It does not need to be proceeded by a [Connect](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/provider-methods/connect)
 event, as it does not require a `session` param.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible#url-structure)

URL structure
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/v1/fungible?token=<fungible>
    

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible#parameters)

Parameters
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`fungible` (required): The [CAIP-19](https://github.com/ChainAgnostic/CAIPs/blob/main/CAIPs/caip-19)
 address of the token page to be viewed, URL-encoded. Defaults to `SOL` if omitted.

[​](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-deeplinks/other-methods/fungible#example)

Example
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    https://phantom.app/ul/v1/fungible?token=solana%3A101%2Faddress%3AFoXyMu5xwXre7zEoSvzViRk3nGawHUp9kUh97y2NDhcq
    

![Fungible Example Gi](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/phantom-deeplinks/images/fungible-example.gif?s=57e4648e5847bbfbcde35961880d6bf9)

# Accounts changed - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/provider-api-reference/events/accounts-changed#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Events

Accounts changed

[Get started](https://docs.phantom.com/introduction)
[Phantom Portal](https://docs.phantom.com/phantom-portal/portal)
[Phantom Connect SDKs](https://docs.phantom.com/wallet-sdks-overview)
[Extension and mobile app](https://docs.phantom.com/solana/integrating-phantom)
[Developer tools and resources](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/overview)

Event emitted upon changing accounts within your Phantom wallet.

Report incorrect code

Copy

Ask AI

    window.ethereum.on('accountsChanged', (newAccounts: String[]) => {
          // "newAccounts" will always be an array, but it can be empty.      
          if (newAccounts) {
            console.log(`switched to new account: ${newAccounts}`);
            accounts = newAccounts;
          } else {
            /**
             * In this case dApps could...
             *
             * 1. Not do anything
             * 2. Only re-connect to the new account if it is trusted
             *
             * ```
             * provider.send('eth_requestAccounts', []).catch((err) => {
             *  // fail silently
             * });
             * ```
             *
             * 3. Always attempt to reconnect
             */
      }
    })
    

You can see an example of [hooking into this event](https://github.com/phantom-labs/eth_sandbox/blob/main/src/App.tsx#L114-L152)
 in our sandbox.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Disconnect](https://docs.phantom.com/ethereum-monad-testnet-base-and-polygon/provider-api-reference/events/disconnect)

# Testnet mode - Phantom developer documentation

[Skip to main content](https://docs.phantom.com/developer-powertools/testnet-mode#content-area)

[Phantom developer documentation home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-light.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=c21a66db70347ca7a31053b98a0b5b0a)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/phantom-e50e2e68/fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9/logo/phantom-dark.svg?fit=max&auto=format&n=fkWrmnMWhjoXSGZ9&q=85&s=af17fb78921412073a894ea97523898c)](https://docs.phantom.com/)
